          <div class="columns-inner">
           <div class="column-center-outer">
            <div class="column-center-inner">
             <div class="main section" id="main" name="Main">
              <div class="widget Blog" id="Blog1">
               <div class="blog-posts hfeed">
                <!-- google_ad_section_start(name=default) -->
                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Saturday, July 30, 2011
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry">
                    <a name="6027351491794322883">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     ~ 4-hearts square (ice cream &amp; cupcakes too) ~
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-6027351491794322883">
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      I wanted to try and come up with a heart square but I couldn't get it to work the way I wanted. I only wanted 1 heart. I was able tofigure outthis 4 hearts square though. Isat down and came up with this pattern all on my own, but it does seem familiar - have any of you ladies &amp; gentlemen ever seen a square like this before? If you have, could you please let me know. Thanks so much. :)
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      **this square measures 5 3/4" - I crocheted it with RHSS and I used a 'J' hook.
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-QQEK3ujD-z0/TjTBwbL13vI/AAAAAAAADOM/13-3WsQMcgI/s1600/heart+square.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-QQEK3ujD-z0/TjTBwbL13vI/AAAAAAAADOM/13-3WsQMcgI/s640/heart+square.jpg" t="" true="" width="609"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      ~~The Butterfly Bush Diaries left me a comment saying that this reminded her of a clover. A few of these squares crocheted in green would make nice potholders for St. Patrick's day.
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Materials:
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      - 4-ply worsted weight acrylic
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      - pink
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      - white
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      - J hook
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Size: Rnds 1 - 5 is approximately 5 3/4" but you can always add more rnds.
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Notes:
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      - I crochet tight so you may need to adjust the size of your crochet hook.
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Directions:
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Rnd 1: With pink ch4, 2 dc in 4th ch from hook, ch 2. (3 dc, ch 2, in same ch) 3 more times. Join with a sl st to top of beginning ch.
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Rnds 2 - 3: Ch 3, dc in each dc around with (2 dc, ch 2, 2 dc) in corner ch-2 spaces.For Rnd 2, join with a sl st to top of beginning ch 3. For Rnd 3, join with a sl st to back loop of the top of beginning ch 3. End off.
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Rnd 4: Join white with a sl st to any corner space, (ch 3, 1 dc, ch 2, 2 dc) in same space. Dc in the back loops of each dc across. Work (2 dc, ch 2, 2 dc) in each corner space. Join with a sl st to top of beginning ch 3.
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cyh7NOCPICU/TjWjgktIHtI/AAAAAAAADOY/DaUQWobkfgM/s1600/DSC08755.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cyh7NOCPICU/TjWjgktIHtI/AAAAAAAADOY/DaUQWobkfgM/s640/DSC08755.JPG" t="" true="" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Rnd 5: Ch 3, dc in each dc around with (2 dc, ch 2, 2 dc) in each corner space around. Join as before.
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      ~~you can end off here or continue to make the square any size that you would like
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      For heart tops:
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Join pink with a sl st to 1st front loop on any side of Rnd 3. *skip next front loop, 3 dc in each of next 2 front loops, skip next front loop, sl st in next front loop. Repeat from * 1 more time. End off.
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Repeat for next 3 sides. Tack down heart tops.
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-HvYEYUJy6MI/TjWjjXDAcXI/AAAAAAAADOc/yQCUyQ-iTJ4/s1600/DSC08756.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-HvYEYUJy6MI/TjWjjXDAcXI/AAAAAAAADOc/yQCUyQ-iTJ4/s640/DSC08756.JPG" t="" true="" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-0c-wAjwqNY0/VaQSdbXxkTI/AAAAAAAAOKQ/j_kEE1CIiCU/s1600/DSC04626.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="426" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-0c-wAjwqNY0/VaQSdbXxkTI/AAAAAAAAOKQ/j_kEE1CIiCU/s640/DSC04626.JPG" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-OTpLT-htE_s/VaQS3ZLJSvI/AAAAAAAAOKY/Kn0-KYA-148/s1600/DSC04631.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="448" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-OTpLT-htE_s/VaQS3ZLJSvI/AAAAAAAAOKY/Kn0-KYA-148/s640/DSC04631.JPG" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      ***Debi Y's pattern***
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       ~~~~~
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Ipp1ZxEuSiw/Tu5Q8jxkvQI/AAAAAAAADvQ/hU49a7Jv1hk/s1600/i+c+cones+sq.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" oda="true" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Ipp1ZxEuSiw/Tu5Q8jxkvQI/AAAAAAAADvQ/hU49a7Jv1hk/s640/i+c+cones+sq.jpg" width="600"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       ~ ice cream cones square ~
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Rnds 1 - 3: with brown, follow Rnds 1 - 3 of '4 hearts square' pattern.
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Rnds 4 - 5: with soft white, follow Rnds 4 - 5 of '4 hearts square' pattern.
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       - you can add a rnd of sc if you'd like.
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       For ice cream tops:
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Row 1: join your color choice with a sl st to 1st front loop on any side of Rnd 3, skip next front loop, 5 dc in next front loop, skip next 2 front loops, sc in next front loop, skip next 2 front loops, 5 dc in next front loop, skip next front loop, sl st in last front loop. Ch 1, turn.
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Row 2: Sl st over to 3rd dc, ch 1, sc in same dc, skip next 2 dc, 5 dc in next sc, skip next 2 dc, sc in next dc, sl st in next 2 dc, sl st in same front loop as beginning sl st of Row 1. End off.
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       - tack down tops of ice cream.
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       ~~~~~
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Fy3PKCnFWYQ/Tu6O12vZ2aI/AAAAAAAADvg/U7dguCObywk/s1600/cupcakes+2.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" oda="true" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Fy3PKCnFWYQ/Tu6O12vZ2aI/AAAAAAAADvg/U7dguCObywk/s640/cupcakes+2.jpg" width="609"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       ~ cupcakes square ~
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Rnd 1: with soft white, follow Rnd 1 of '4 hearts square' pattern.
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Rnds 2 - 3: with brown, follow Rnds 2 - 3 of '4 hearts square' pattern.
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Rnds 4 -5: with soft white, follow Rnds4 - 5 of '4 hearts square' pattern.
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       - you can add a rnd of sc if you'd like
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       For cupcake tops:
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Rows 1 - 2: follow Rows 1 - 2 of ice cream tops.
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       - tack down tops of cupcakes
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       - I used Sharpie permanent markers to makethe sprinkles
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       ***Debi Y's pattern***
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       <br/>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>

      var config = {'blogId': '498281580416888164', 'postId': '6027351491794322883', 'feed': 'http://hooksandyarns.blogspot.com/feeds/6027351491794322883/comments/default', 'authorName': 'Debi Y.', 'authorUrl': 'http://www.blogger.com/profile/08879733455358400724', 'baseUri': 'http://www.blogger.com', 'maxThreadDepth': 2};

      var cursor = null;
      if (items &amp;&amp; items.length &gt; 0) {
        cursor = parseInt(items[items.length - 1].timestamp) + 1;
      }

      var bodyFromEntry = function(entry) {
        if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
          for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.contentRemoved') {
              return '&lt;span class="deleted-comment"&gt;' + entry.content.$t + '&lt;/span&gt;';
            }
          }
        }
        return entry.content.$t;
      }

      var parse = function(data) {
        cursor = null;
        var comments = [];
        if (data &amp;&amp; data.feed &amp;&amp; data.feed.entry) {
          for (var i = 0, entry; entry = data.feed.entry[i]; i++) {
            var comment = {};
            // comment ID, parsed out of the original id format
            var id = /blog-(\d+).post-(\d+)/.exec(entry.id.$t);
            comment.id = id ? id[2] : null;
            comment.body = bodyFromEntry(entry);
            comment.timestamp = Date.parse(entry.published.$t) + '';
            if (entry.author &amp;&amp; entry.author.constructor === Array) {
              var auth = entry.author[0];
              if (auth) {
                comment.author = {
                  name: (auth.name ? auth.name.$t : undefined),
                  profileUrl: (auth.uri ? auth.uri.$t : undefined),
                  avatarUrl: (auth.gd$image ? auth.gd$image.src : undefined)
                };
              }
            }
            if (entry.link) {
              if (entry.link[2]) {
                comment.link = comment.permalink = entry.link[2].href;
              }
              if (entry.link[3]) {
                var pid = /.*comments\/default\/(\d+)\?.*/.exec(entry.link[3].href);
                if (pid &amp;&amp; pid[1]) {
                  comment.parentId = pid[1];
                }
              }
            }
            comment.deleteclass = 'item-control blog-admin';
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
              for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
                if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.itemClass') {
                  comment.deleteclass += ' ' + entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                } else if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.displayTime') {
                  comment.displayTime = entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                }
              }
            }
            comments.push(comment);
          }
        }
        return comments;
      };

      var paginator = function(callback) {
        if (hasMore()) {
          var url = config.feed + '?alt=json&amp;v=2&amp;orderby=published&amp;reverse=false&amp;max-results=50';
          if (cursor) {
            url += '&amp;published-min=' + new Date(cursor).toISOString();
          }
          window.bloggercomments = function(data) {
            var parsed = parse(data);
            cursor = parsed.length &lt; 50 ? null
                : parseInt(parsed[parsed.length - 1].timestamp) + 1
            callback(parsed);
            window.bloggercomments = null;
          }
          url += '&amp;callback=bloggercomments';
          var script = document.createElement('script');
          script.type = 'text/javascript';
          script.src = url;
          document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
        }
      };
      var hasMore = function() {
        return !!cursor;
      };
      var getMeta = function(key, comment) {
        if ('iswriter' == key) {
          var matches = !!comment.author
              &amp;&amp; comment.author.name == config.authorName
              &amp;&amp; comment.author.profileUrl == config.authorUrl;
          return matches ? 'true' : '';
        } else if ('deletelink' == key) {
          return config.baseUri + '/delete-comment.g?blogID='
               + config.blogId + '&amp;postID=' + comment.id;
        } else if ('deleteclass' == key) {
          return comment.deleteclass;
        }
        return '';
      };

      var replybox = null;
      var replyUrlParts = null;
      var replyParent = undefined;

      var onReply = function(commentId, domId) {
        if (replybox == null) {
          // lazily cache replybox, and adjust to suit this style:
          replybox = document.getElementById('comment-editor');
          if (replybox != null) {
            replybox.height = '250px';
            replybox.style.display = 'block';
            replyUrlParts = replybox.src.split('#');
          }
        }
        if (replybox &amp;&amp; (commentId !== replyParent)) {
          document.getElementById(domId).insertBefore(replybox, null);
          replybox.src = replyUrlParts[0]
              + (commentId ? '&amp;parentID=' + commentId : '')
              + '#' + replyUrlParts[1];
          replyParent = commentId;
        }
      };

      var hash = (window.location.hash || '#').substring(1);
      var startThread, targetComment;
      if (/^comment-form_/.test(hash)) {
        startThread = hash.substring('comment-form_'.length);
      } else if (/^c[0-9]+$/.test(hash)) {
        targetComment = hash.substring(1);
      }

      // Configure commenting API:
      var configJso = {
        'maxDepth': config.maxThreadDepth
      };
      var provider = {
        'id': config.postId,
        'data': items,
        'loadNext': paginator,
        'hasMore': hasMore,
        'getMeta': getMeta,
        'onReply': onReply,
        'rendered': true,
        'initComment': targetComment,
        'initReplyThread': startThread,
        'config': configJso,
        'messages': msgs
      };

      var render = function() {
        if (window.goog &amp;&amp; window.goog.comments) {
          var holder = document.getElementById('comment-holder');
          window.goog.comments.render(holder, provider);
        }
      };

      // render now, or queue to render when library loads:
      if (window.goog &amp;&amp; window.goog.comments) {
        render();
      } else {
        window.goog = window.goog || {};
        window.goog.comments = window.goog.comments || {};
        window.goog.comments.loadQueue = window.goog.comments.loadQueue || [];
        window.goog.comments.loadQueue.push(render);
      }
    })();

                             <br/>
                             AnitraX - I made my crochet hooks with polymer clay.  I posted about it on July 6th.  Here's the link -
                             <br/>
                             <br/>
                             http://hooksandyarns.blogspot.com/2011/07/re-post-for-heldasland.html

                                  <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_73MC">
                                   Hi anonymous.
                                   <br/>
                                   <br/>
                                   1) if you would prefer, you can ch 2 and then work a dc in the same space as the ch 2.  Just remember not to count the ch 2 as a dc.
                                   <br/>
                                   <br/>
                                   2)  yes seriously.  you will weave in the ends just like any other crochet project.
                                   <br/>
                                   <br/>
                                   3)  I tack down the middle dc of each top of the hearts with a separate piece of yarn.  You can then tie the ends into a knot and weave them in.
                                  </p>

                  do
                 </strong>

                  not
                 </strong>

                <h2 class="title">
                 Followers
                </h2>
                <div class="widget-content">
                 <div id="Followers1-wrapper">
                  <div style="margin-right:2px;">
                   <div>
                    <script src="https://apis.google.com/js/plusone.js" type="text/javascript">
                    </script>
                    <div id="followers-iframe-container">
                    </div>
                    <script type="text/javascript">
                     window.followersIframe = null;
    function followersIframeOpen(url) {
      gapi.load("gapi.iframes", function() {
        if (gapi.iframes &amp;&amp; gapi.iframes.getContext) {
          window.followersIframe = gapi.iframes.getContext().openChild({
            url: url,
            where: document.getElementById("followers-iframe-container"),
            messageHandlersFilter: gapi.iframes.CROSS_ORIGIN_IFRAMES_FILTER,
            messageHandlers: {
              '_ready': function(obj) {
                window.followersIframe.getIframeEl().height = obj.height;
              },
              'reset': function() {
                window.followersIframe.close();
                followersIframeOpen("https://www.blogger.com/followers.g?blogID\x3d498281580416888164\x26origin\x3dhttp://hooksandyarns.blogspot.com/\x26colors\x3dCgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudBILdHJhbnNwYXJlbnQaBjYwNjA2MCIGYjMyYzIwKgZmZmZmZmYyBjAwMDAwMDoGNjA2MDYwQgZiMzJjMjBKBjk2OTY5NlIGYjMyYzIwWgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudA%3D%3D\x26postID\x3d6027351491794322883");
              },
              'open': function(url) {
                window.followersIframe.close();
                followersIframeOpen(url);
              }
            }
          });
        }
      });
    }
